=========================================================================
write-tags-from-csv.py ver 0.66  updated Fri 10 Aug 2023 18:25:00 PM CDT 
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 
This Python program embeds IPTC metadata tags into TIFF and JPEG files
listed in a CSV file generated from the HST PDB.
 
To run correctly, it requires the following in the current working directory: 
 
 (1) the PDB CSV file with updated IPTC headers
 (2) the TIFF or JPEG files listed in the CSV file
 (3) the Python program [ write-tags-from-csv.py ] 
 
Free disk space on current drive: 851632 MB
 
Number of lines in the CSV file: 2821
 
Number of jpg files in the diretory:  0
 
=========================================================================
 
Press Enter to continue...
